<main id="main" role="main">
<span id="main-content" tabindex="-1"></span>
<div class="layout-content">
<div class="region region-content">
<div class="block block-system block-system-main-block" id="block-ruhlamat-content">
<div class="layout layout--onecol">
<div class="layout__region layout__region--content">
<div class="field field--name-node-title field--type-ds field--label-hidden field__item"><h1 class="page-title">
  Traditional Special Machinery
</h1>
</div>
<div class="field field--name-field-paragraphs field--type-entity-reference-revisions field--label-hidden field__items">
<div class="field__item">
<div class="paragraph paragraph--type--blockquote paragraph--view-mode--default">
<blockquote class="field field--name-field-blockquote field--type-text-long field--label-hidden field__item"><p>Founded out of the tradition-steeped "Uhren- und Maschinenfabrik Ruhla", ruhlamat GmbH was established in 1991.</p></blockquote>
</div></div>
<div class="field__item">
<div class="paragraph paragraph--type--full-width-text paragraph--view-mode--default">
<div class="clearfix text-formatted field field--name-field-text-full-width field--type-text-long field--label-hidden field__item"><p>As a <strong>longstanding specialist in the field of specialised machine construction</strong>, ruhlamat offers you individually tailored as well as standardised machine solutions. Our aim is to provide you with precise tools in order to sustainably boost the success of your company.</p>
<p><strong>Customer-specific and unique machine solutions</strong> as well as <strong>standardised, complete turnkey solutions</strong> and systems are what you get at ruhlamat. They are used for example in the automotive and electronic industry, medicine and packaging area as well as in the manufacturing and personalisation of ID and smart cards as well as passports. <a data-entity-substitution="canonical" data-entity-type="node" data-entity-uuid="3ab007c8-f5a2-49b8-a140-c7728aeb933b" href="/en/company/about-us" title="About Us">Learn more about ruhlamat</a></p></div>
</div></div>
